var prob = randomNumber(1, 8);
if (prob>=8) {
  prob = prob-randomNumber(0,7);
}

                                  if (crit2*n>=1e6) {
                                  text(Math.round(crit2*n/1e3)/1e3+"M"+"!", 200, 50);
                              } else {
                                  text(Math.round(crit2)*n+"!", 200, 50);
                              }
                                }
                              }else{
                                textSize(25);
                                fill("white");
                                text("MISSED", 200, 50);
                              }
                            }else{

                              fill("white");

                                  }
                                }
                              }else{
                                text("MISSED", 200, 50);
                              }
                            }
                            cooldown = cooldown-1;
                          }
                              } else {

                            fly.x = 1e100;
                            fli = fli-7

                }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
    }
  if (fly.y<frog.y){
    fly.y = fly.y+0.6;
  }
  if (fly.y>frog.y){
    fly.y = fly.y-0.6;
  }
  if (keyDown("left")) {
    if (frog.x>15) {
      frog.x = frog.x-1.6;
    }
      }
  if (keyDown("right")) {
    if (frog.x<385) {
      frog.x = frog.x+1.6;
    }
  }
  if (keyDown("Up")) {
    if (frog.y>15) {
      frog.y = frog.y-1.6;
    }
  }
  if (keyDown("Down")) {
    if (frog.y<385) {
      frog.y = frog.y+1.6;
    }
  }
  if (keyDown("left")) {
    if (keyDown("Up")) {
      frog.x = frog.x-1.6/Math.pow(2,1/2)+1.6;
      frog.y = frog.y-1.6/Math.pow(2,1/2)+1.6;
    }
  }
  if (keyDown("left")) {
    if (keyDown("Down")) {
      frog.x = frog.x-1.6/Math.pow(2,1/2)+1.6;
      frog.y = frog.y+1.6/Math.pow(2,1/2)-1.6;
    }
  }
  if (keyDown("right")) {
    if (keyDown("Up")) {
      frog.x = frog.x+1.6/Math.pow(2,1/2)-1.6;
      frog.y = frog.y-1.6/Math.pow(2,1/2)+1.6;
    }
  }
  if (keyDown("right")) {
    if (keyDown("Down")) {
      frog.x = frog.x+1.6/Math.pow(2,1/2)-1.6;
      frog.y = frog.y+1.6/Math.pow(2,1/2)-1.6;
    }
  }
  if (fly.x<frog.x){
    fly.x = fly.x+0.6;
  }
  if (fly.x>frog.x){
    fly.x = fly.x-0.6;
  }
  if (fly.y>frog.y){
    if (fly.x>frog.x){
    fly.x = fly.x+0.6-0.6/Math.pow(2,1/2);
    fly.y = fly.y+0.6-0.6/Math.pow(2,1/2);
  }
  }if (fly.y>frog.y){
    if (fly.x<frog.x){
    fly.x = fly.x-0.6+0.6/Math.pow(2,1/2);
    fly.y = fly.y+0.6-0.6/Math.pow(2,1/2);
  }
  }if (fly.y<frog.y){
    if (fly.x>frog.x){
    fly.x = fly.x+0.6-0.6/Math.pow(2,1/2);
    fly.y = fly.y-0.6+0.6/Math.pow(2,1/2);
  }
  }if (fly.y<frog.y){
    if (fly.x<frog.x){
    fly.x = fly.x-0.6+0.6/Math.pow(2,1/2);
    fly.y = fly.y-0.6+0.6/Math.pow(2,1/2);
  }
  }
  textSize(30);
